mysql> -- To include inactive reviewers  use LEFT JOIN since there are reviewers in that table that do not have corresponding reviews in the reviews table, which is currently to thr right of the JION stmt
mysql> 
mysql> SELECT reviewers.first_name, 
    ->        reviewers.last_name,
    ->        COUNT(reviews.rating),
    ->        MIN(reviews.rating),
    ->        MAX(reviews.rating),
    ->        AVG(reviews.rating),
    -> CASE
    ->     WHEN COUNT(reviews.rating) = 0 THEN 'INACTIVE' 
    ->     ELSE 'ACTIVE' 
    -> END AS 'STATUS'  
    -> FROM reviewers       
    -> LEFT JOIN reviews
    ->     ON reviewers.id = reviews.reviewer_id
    -> GROUP BY reviewers.id;
+------------+-----------+-----------------------+---------------------+---------------------+---------------------+----------+
| first_name | last_name | COUNT(reviews.rating) | MIN(reviews.rating) | MAX(reviews.rating) | AVG(reviews.rating) | STATUS   |
+------------+-----------+-----------------------+---------------------+---------------------+---------------------+----------+
| Thomas     | Stoneman  |                     5 |                 7.0 |                 9.5 |             8.02000 | ACTIVE   |
| Wyatt      | Skaggs    |                     9 |                 5.5 |                 9.3 |             7.80000 | ACTIVE   |
| Kimbra     | Masters   |                     9 |                 6.8 |                 9.0 |             7.98889 | ACTIVE   |
| Domingo    | Cortes    |                    10 |                 5.8 |                 9.1 |             7.83000 | ACTIVE   |
| Colt       | Steele    |                    10 |                 4.5 |                 9.9 |             8.77000 | ACTIVE   |
| Pinkie     | Petit     |                     4 |                 4.3 |                 8.8 |             7.25000 | ACTIVE   |

mysql> SELECT reviewers.first_name, 
    ->        reviewers.last_name,
    ->        COUNT(reviews.rating) AS 'COUNT',
    ->        MIN(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)) AS 'MIN',
    ->        MAX(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)) AS 'MAX',
    ->        AVG(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)) AS 'AVG',
    -> CASE
    ->     WHEN COUNT(reviews.rating) = 0 THEN 'INACTIVE' 
    ->     ELSE 'ACTIVE' 
    -> END AS 'STATUS'  
    -> FROM reviewers       
    -> LEFT JOIN reviews
    ->     ON reviewers.id = reviews.reviewer_id
    -> GROUP BY reviewers.id;

mysql> -- ok no problem using reserved words as aliases
mysql> -- One last thing: use ROUND 
mysql> 
mysql> SELECT reviewers.first_name, 
    ->        reviewers.last_name,
    ->        COUNT(reviews.rating) AS COUNT,
    ->        ROUND(MIN(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS MIN,
    ->        ROUND(MAX(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS MAX,
    ->        ROUND(AVG(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS AVG,
    -> CASE
    ->     WHEN COUNT(reviews.rating) = 0 THEN 'INACTIVE' 
    ->     ELSE 'ACTIVE' 
    -> END AS 'STATUS'  
    -> FROM reviewers       
    -> LEFT JOIN reviews
    ->     ON reviewers.id = reviews.reviewer_id
    -> GROUP BY reviewers.id;
+------------+-----------+-------+------+------+------+----------+
| first_name | last_name | COUNT | MIN  | MAX  | AVG  | STATUS   |

| Wyatt      | Skaggs    |     9 | 5.50 | 9.30 | 7.80 | ACTIVE   |

mysql> -- that looks better
mysql> -- you can add some complexity to above table. Say, call a reviewer with avg ratings given above 8 as fair critique. Else harsh critique etc.
mysql> 
mysql> 
mysql> SELECT reviewers.first_name, 
    ->        reviewers.last_name,
    ->        COUNT(reviews.rating) AS COUNT,
    ->        ROUND(MIN(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS MIN,
    ->        ROUND(MAX(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS MAX,
    ->        ROUND(AVG(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS AVG,
    -> CASE
    ->     WHEN COUNT(reviews.rating) = 0 THEN 'INACTIVE' 
    ->     ELSE 'ACTIVE' 
    -> END AS 'STATUS'  
    -> CASE
    ->     WHEN AVG(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0))>8.00 THEN 'FAIR CRITIQUE' 
    ->     ELSE  'HARSH CRITIQUE'
    ->     END AS 'Rviewer Class'
    -> FROM reviewers       
    -> LEFT JOIN reviews
    ->     ON reviewers.id = reviews.reviewer_id
    -> GROUP BY reviewers.id;
ERROR 1064 (42000): You have an error in your SQL syntax; check the manual that corresponds to your MySQL server version for the right syntax to use near 'CASE
    WHEN AVG(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0))>8.00 THEN 'FAIR CRITIQUE' 
    ELSE ' at line 11

mysql> -- Another big lesson: Use a comma to separate multiple CASE clauses.
mysql> -- we have a small problem in above table that an INACTIVE reviewer is called HARSH. Fix it. There seems to be many ways to do it. Try to apply the simplest one.
mysql> 
mysql> SELECT reviewers.first_name, 
    ->        reviewers.last_name,
    ->        COUNT(reviews.rating) AS COUNT,
    ->        ROUND(MIN(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS MIN,
    ->        ROUND(MAX(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS MAX,
    ->        ROUND(AVG(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS AVG,
    -> CASE
    ->     WHEN COUNT(reviews.rating) = 0 THEN 'INACTIVE' 
    ->     ELSE 'ACTIVE' 
    -> END AS 'STATUS',
    -> CASE
    ->     WHEN AVG(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0))>8 THEN 'FAIR CRITIQUE' 
    ->     WHEN AVG(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0))<8 AND COUNT(reviews.rating) != 0  THEN 'HARSH CRITIQUE'
    ->     ELSE  'NOT A CRITIQUE'
    ->     END AS 'Rviewer Class'
    -> FROM reviewers       
    -> LEFT JOIN reviews
    ->     ON reviewers.id = reviews.reviewer_id
    -> GROUP BY reviewers.id;
+------------+-----------+-------+------+------+------+----------+----------------+
| first_name | last_name | COUNT | MIN  | MAX  | AVG  | STATUS   | Rviewer Class  |
+------------+-----------+-------+------+------+------+----------+----------------+
| Thomas     | Stoneman  |     5 | 7.00 | 9.50 | 8.02 | ACTIVE   | FAIR CRITIQUE  |
| Wyatt      | Skaggs    |     9 | 5.50 | 9.30 | 7.80 | ACTIVE   | HARSH CRITIQUE |
| Kimbra     | Masters   |     9 | 6.80 | 9.00 | 7.99 | ACTIVE   | HARSH CRITIQUE |
| Domingo    | Cortes    |    10 | 5.80 | 9.10 | 7.83 | ACTIVE   | HARSH CRITIQUE |
| Colt       | Steele    |    10 | 4.50 | 9.90 | 8.77 | ACTIVE   | FAIR CRITIQUE  |
| Pinkie     | Petit     |     4 | 4.30 | 8.80 | 7.25 | ACTIVE   | HARSH CRITIQUE |
| Marlon     | Crafford  |     0 | 0.00 | 0.00 | 0.00 | INACTIVE | NOT A CRITIQUE |
+------------+-----------+-------+------+------+------+----------+----------------+
7 rows in set (0.00 sec)

mysql> -- Wondering which is more efficient: 'AVG(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0))' or 'IFNULL(AVG(reviews.rating),0)'? probably the latter. Not time to test. Move on!
mysql> -- A wonderful tip from the instructor. Use IF(...) as STATUS instead of CASE. Going to do it.
mysql> 
mysql> 
mysql> 
mysql> 
mysql> # MAKE IT MORE COMPLEX use IF instead of CASE
mysql> SELECT reviewers.first_name, 
    ->        reviewers.last_name,
    ->        COUNT(reviews.rating) AS COUNT,
    ->        ROUND(MIN(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS MIN,
    ->        ROUND(MAX(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS MAX,
    ->        ROUND(AVG(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS AVG,
    ->        IF COUNT(reviews.rating) = 0 , 'INACTIVE','ACTIVE') AS 'STATUS',
    -> CASE
    ->     WHEN COUNT(reviews.rating) != 0 
    ->          AVG(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0))>8, 'FAIR CRITIQUE','HARSH CRITIQUE') 
    ->     ELSE  'NOT A CRITIQUE'
    ->     END AS 'Rviewer Class'
    -> FROM reviewers       
    -> LEFT JOIN reviews
    ->     ON reviewers.id = reviews.reviewer_id
    -> GROUP BY reviewers.id;
ERROR 1064 (42000): You have an error in your SQL syntax; check the manual that corresponds to your MySQL server version for the right syntax to use near 'COUNT(reviews.rating) = 0 , 'INACTIVE','ACTIVE') AS 'STATUS',
CASE
    WHEN COUN' at line 7

mysql> # MAKE IT MORE COMPLEX use IF instead of CASE
mysql> SELECT reviewers.first_name, 
    ->        reviewers.last_name,
    ->        COUNT(reviews.rating) AS COUNT,
    ->        ROUND(MIN(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS MIN,

mysql> -- Remember no comma after the last element of select before the FROM. Unlike CASE.
mysql> 
mysql> 
mysql> # MAKE IT MORE COMPLEX use IF instead of CASE + ADD CRITIQUE TYPES
mysql> SELECT reviewers.first_name, 
    ->        reviewers.last_name,
    ->        COUNT(reviews.rating) AS COUNT,
    ->        ROUND(MIN(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS MIN,
    ->        ROUND(MAX(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS MAX,
    ->        ROUND(AVG(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS AVG,
    ->        IF (COUNT(reviews.rating) = 0 , 'INACTIVE','ACTIVE') AS 'STATUS'
    ->        IF (IFNULL(AVG(reviews.rating),0) >8 , 'FAIR CRITIQUE','HARSH CRITIQUE') AS 'STATUS'
    ->        
    -> FROM reviewers       
    -> LEFT JOIN reviews

mysql> -- LESSON: For more than 2 cases IF won't help. Go back to CASE!
mysql> 
mysql> SELECT reviewers.first_name, 
    ->        reviewers.last_name,
    ->        COUNT(reviews.rating) AS COUNT,
    ->        ROUND(MIN(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS MIN,
    ->        ROUND(MAX(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS MAX,
    ->        ROUND(AVG(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0)),2) AS AVG,
    -> CASE
    ->     WHEN COUNT(reviews.rating) = 0 THEN 'INACTIVE' 
    ->     ELSE 'ACTIVE' 
    -> END AS 'STATUS',
    -> CASE
    ->     WHEN AVG(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0))>8 THEN 'FAIR CRITIQUE' 
    ->     WHEN AVG(IFNULL(reviews.rating,0))<8 AND COUNT(reviews.rating) != 0  THEN 'HARSH CRITIQUE'
    ->     ELSE  'NOT A CRITIQUE'
    ->     END AS 'Rviewer Class'
    -> FROM reviewers       
    -> LEFT JOIN reviews
    ->     ON reviewers.id = reviews.reviewer_id
    -> GROUP BY reviewers.id;
+------------+-----------+-------+------+------+------+----------+----------------+
| first_name | last_name | COUNT | MIN  | MAX  | AVG  | STATUS   | Rviewer Class  |
+------------+-----------+-------+------+------+------+----------+----------------+
| Thomas     | Stoneman  |     5 | 7.00 | 9.50 | 8.02 | ACTIVE   | FAIR CRITIQUE  |
| Wyatt      | Skaggs    |     9 | 5.50 | 9.30 | 7.80 | ACTIVE   | HARSH CRITIQUE |
| Kimbra     | Masters   |     9 | 6.80 | 9.00 | 7.99 | ACTIVE   | HARSH CRITIQUE |
| Domingo    | Cortes    |    10 | 5.80 | 9.10 | 7.83 | ACTIVE   | HARSH CRITIQUE |
| Colt       | Steele    |    10 | 4.50 | 9.90 | 8.77 | ACTIVE   | FAIR CRITIQUE  |
| Pinkie     | Petit     |     4 | 4.30 | 8.80 | 7.25 | ACTIVE   | HARSH CRITIQUE |
| Marlon     | Crafford  |     0 | 0.00 | 0.00 | 0.00 | INACTIVE | NOT A CRITIQUE |
+------------+-----------+-------+------+------+------+----------+----------------+
7 rows in set (0.00 sec)

   /*>     */
    ->     user_id INT NOT NULL,
    ->     photo_id INT NOT NULL,
    ->     created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    ->     PRIMARY KEY(user_id, photo_id),
    ->     FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    ->     FOREIGN KEY(photo_id) REFERENCES photos(id) 
    -> );
Query OK, 0 rows affected (0.12 sec)

mysql> 
mysql> 
mysql> -- who got the most likes on a single photo post?
mysql> SELECT 
    ->        photos.id, 
    ->        users.username, 
    ->        likes.user_id, 
    ->        likes.photo_id,
    ->        count(*) as 'like count' 
    -> FROM  photos
    -> JOIN  users
    ->     ON photos.user_id = users.id
    -> JOIN likes
    ->     ON likes.photo_id = photos.id
    ->     GROUP BY likes.photo_id;

mysql> -- who got the most likes on a single photo post?
mysql> SELECT 
    ->        photos.id, 
    ->        users.username, 
    ->        likes.user_id, 
    ->        likes.photo_id,
    ->        count(*) as 'like count' 
    -> FROM  photos
    -> JOIN  users
    ->     ON photos.user_id = users.id
    -> JOIN likes
    ->     ON likes.photo_id = photos.id
    ->     GROUP BY likes.photo_id, users.id;

mysql> -- who got the most likes on a single photo post?
mysql> SELECT 
    ->        users.username, 
    ->        likes.user_id, 
    ->        likes.photo_id,
    ->        count(*) as 'like count' 
    -> FROM  photos
    -> JOIN  users
    ->     ON photos.user_id = users.id
    -> JOIN likes
    ->     ON likes.photo_id = photos.id
    ->     GROUP BY likes.photo_id, users.id;

mysql> -- who got the most likes on a single photo post?
mysql> SELECT 
    ->        users.username, 
    ->        likes.user_id, 
    ->        likes.photo_id,
    ->        count(*) as 'like count' 
    -> FROM  photos
    -> JOIN  users
    ->     ON photos.user_id = users.id
    -> JOIN likes
    ->     ON likes.photo_id = photos.id
    ->     GROUP BY likes.photo_id, photos.user_id ;

mysql> -- who got the most likes on a single photo post?
mysql> SELECT 
    ->        users.username, 
    ->        likes.user_id, 
    ->        likes.photo_id,
    ->        count(likes.photo_id) as 'like count' 
    -> FROM  photos
    -> JOIN  users
    ->     ON photos.user_id = users.id
    -> JOIN likes
    ->     ON likes.photo_id = photos.id
    ->     GROUP BY likes.photo_id, photos.user_id ;

mysql> -- who got the most likes on a single photo post?
mysql> SELECT 
    ->        users.id,
    ->        users.username, 
    ->        likes.user_id, 
    ->        likes.photo_id,
    ->        count(likes.photo_id) as 'like count' 
    -> FROM  photos
    -> JOIN  users
    ->     ON photos.user_id = users.id
    -> JOIN likes
    ->     ON likes.photo_id = photos.id
    ->     GROUP BY likes.photo_id, photos.user_id ;

mysql> -- who got the most likes on a single photo post?
mysql> SELECT 
    ->        users.id,
    ->        users.username, 
    ->        likes.user_id, 
    ->        likes.photo_id,
    ->        count(likes.photo_id) as like_counts 
    -> FROM  photos
    -> JOIN  users
    ->     ON photos.user_id = users.id
    -> JOIN likes
    ->     ON likes.photo_id = photos.id
    ->     GROUP BY likes.photo_id, photos.user_id 
    ->     ORDER BY like_counts desc;

mysql> -- who got the most likes on a single photo post?
mysql> SELECT 
    ->        users.id,
    ->        users.username, 
    ->        likes.photo_id,
    ->        count(likes.photo_id) as like_counts 
    -> FROM  photos
    -> JOIN  users
    ->     ON photos.user_id = users.id
    -> JOIN likes
    ->     ON likes.photo_id = photos.id
    ->     GROUP BY likes.photo_id, photos.user_id 
    ->     ORDER BY like_counts desc;

mysql> -- who got the most likes on a single photo post?
mysql> SELECT 
    ->        users.id,
    ->        users.username, 
    ->        likes.photo_id,
    ->        count(likes.photo_id) as like_counts,
    ->        CONCAT('The winner of most likes per single photo is ', users.username, 
    ->                  ' for his photo with an id of ', photos.id, ', which managed ', like_counts, ' likes.')
    -> FROM  photos
    -> JOIN  users
    ->     ON photos.user_id = users.id
    -> JOIN likes
    ->     ON likes.photo_id = photos.id
    ->     GROUP BY likes.photo_id, photos.user_id 
    ->     ORDER BY like_counts desc
    ->     LIMIT 1;
ERROR 1054 (42S22): Unknown column 'like_counts' in 'field list'

mysql> -- who got the most likes on a single photo post?
mysql> SELECT 
    ->  /*      users.id,
   /*>        users.username, 
   /*>        likes.photo_id,
   /*>        count(likes.photo_id) as like_counts,
   /*>  */      
    ->        CONCAT('The winner of most likes per single photo is ', users.username, ' (user id ', users.id,')',
    ->                  ' for his photo ', photos.image_url, ', which managed ', count(likes.photo_id), ' likes. The photo id is ', photos.id) AS winner
    -> FROM  photos
    -> JOIN  users
    ->     ON photos.user_id = users.id
    -> JOIN likes

mysql> SELECT 
    ->        users.id,
    ->        users.username,
    ->        count(users.id) as like_counts
    -> FROM  photos
    -> JOIN  users
    ->     ON photos.user_id = users.id
    -> JOIN likes
    ->     ON likes.photo_id = photos.id
    ->     GROUP BY likes.photo_id, photos.user_id 
    ->     ORDER BY count(users.id) desc;
